Version 2.0		 Testing 14-Nov-08 0                 Need to formally test the excel loader to ensure it works according to expectations and instructions.

The instructions for importing excel sheets are here: https://wiki.nci.nih.gov/display/CTMS/caAERS+Excel+Data+Import
You can download the good xl sheets here: https://gforge.nci.nih.gov/svnroot/caaersappdev/trunk/projects/excelstudyloader/src/main/resources/samples/Mayo-22-protocols-v1.xls

The following scenarios should be tested at a minimum:
- ensure all the data in the Excel loader is loaded and loaded correctly (clearly document any gaps or exceptions)
- test what happens if the excel loader is re-run
- test that unallowed duplicates are handled properly (duplicate studies, investigators, tacs, agents, etc)
- test the constraints regarding editing the Excel file, the format supported (ie. Office 2003-2007, Mac, etc). This is to see how finicky the Excel formating is for proper use of the feature.

caAERS CAAERS-1320 Meddra Disease terminology version issues Improvement Open Major UNRESOLVED monish.dombla karthik.iyer@semanticbits.com 11/6/2008 12:05 11/19/2008 11:58 Version 1.5 Version 1.5 Module 2: Integration with local CTMS systems 5-Dec-08 0               caAERS v. 1.5.2-SNAPSHOT (2008-11-06 10:25:26) '-- This is a fairly critical issue and it needs to be sorted out with a meeting with all concerned parties, i.e
karthik, biju, paul,monish, sameer, jennifer and ram.

The following is the scenario:
1> Import study into caaers using study XML.
2> This study is of has meddra diseases.
3> The study is imported successfully
4> user searches for study and goes into edit study flow
5> User goes to disease tab. An error page is shown [error pasted below]
6> This is happening because the meddra version is not mentioned in the study details tab.
7> This is because the study XML does not have a tag for meddra version
8> However it is not possible to add a tag because the meddra version cannot be specified as enum [like CTC version are specified]
9> This is because in the UI when meddra versions are loaded the meddra version is specified as free form text.
10>Using enums is possible only when meddra versions are auto-numbered as they are uploaded into caaers
11> This is not possible because the meddra files which are imported do not have version information in them.
